## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology
**Analysis**: Population growth rate is modeled based on time and population size, which falls under the realm of population ecology, focusing on the dynamics and modeling of population changes over time.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Logistic growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K) (logistic growth model with carrying capacity K)
- Gompertz growth: dP/dt = r * P * ln(K / P) (Gompertz growth model for population growth)
- Linear growth: dP/dt = r * P (linear growth model for population increase)
- Exponential growth: dP/dt = r * P (exponential growth model for rapid population increase)
- Verhulst growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K) / (1 + c * P / K) (Verhulst model with competition factor c)
- Skellam growth: dP/dt = r * P * exp(-c * P) (Skellam model for diffusion-controlled growth)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics (discrete population model): dP/dt = r * S / (S + K) (modified Michaelis-Menten kinetics for population growth)
- Power-law growth: dP/dt = r * P**c (power-law model for rapid population growth)
- Abrupt growth: dP/dt = r * P / (1 + c * P) (model for rapid population growth with saturation)
- Heaviside step growth: dP/dt = r * P / (1 + exp(c * (P - K))) (model for abrupt growth with carrying capacity K)
- Cheng growth: dP/dt = r * P * sqrt(1 - P / K) (Cheng model for population growth with carrying capacity K)
- Heaps growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K)**c (Heaps model for population growth with carrying capacity K and competition factor c)
- Coble growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K)**2 (Coble model for population growth with carrying capacity K)
- Li-Steffensen growth: dP/dt = r * P * sqrt(K / P) (Li-Steffensen model for population growth with carrying capacity K)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Growth/decay oscillation → Power-law growth: dP/dt = r * P**c (rapid growth or decay with oscillation)
- Carrying capacity effects → Logistic growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K) (population growth with saturation at carrying capacity K)
- Threshold/activation behavior → Heaviside step growth: dP/dt = r * P / (1 + exp(c * (P - K))) (abrupt growth with carrying capacity K)
- Cross-interaction between population and time → Michaelis-Menten kinetics: dP/dt = r * S / (S + K) (population growth with interaction between population size and time)
- Population saturation with decaying rate → Heaps growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K)**c (population growth with carrying capacity K and decaying rate c)
- Sigmoidal growth with inflection point → Gompertz growth: dP/dt = r * P * ln(K / P) (sigmoidal growth model for population increase)
- Population growth with interaction between populations → Skellam growth: dP/dt = r * P * exp(-c * P) (diffusion-controlled growth model for population interaction)
- Population growth with abrupt change in growth rate → Coble growth: dP/dt = r * P * (1 - P / K)**2 (population growth with abrupt change in growth rate)
- Population growth with square-root law → Cheng growth: dP/dt = r * P * sqrt(1 - P / K) (population growth with square-root law)
- Population growth with power-law law → Power-law growth: dP/dt = r * P**c (population growth with power-law law)
- Population growth with decaying rate → Heaviside step growth: dP/dt = r * P / (1 + exp(c * (P - K))) (population growth with decaying rate)
